No model worked, all NO_TRADE\n            signals[:] = -1\n            return signals\n\n        probas_array = np.array(probas_matrix)  # shape: (n_models, n_samples)\n\n        # Average confidence for each sample\n        avg_proba = probas_array.mean(axis=0)\n\n        # Count models predicting UP\n        up_votes = (probas_array >= 0.5).sum(axis=0)\n\n        down_votes = len(probas_matrix) - up_votes\n\n        # Apply gating rules\n        for i, (avg_p, up, down) in enumerate(zip(avg_proba, up_votes, down_votes)):\n            # Check agreement\n            if up >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 1\n                confidence = avg_p\n            elif down >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 0\n                confidence = 1 - avg_p  # confidence in DOWN is 1 - avg_proba\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n                continue\n\n            # Check confidence threshold\n            if confidence >= self.min_confidence:\n                signals.iloc[i] = direction\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n\n        return signals\n\n    def adjust_thresholds(\n        self,\n        recent_performance: Dict[str, float],\n        target_sharpe: float = 1.0,\n        target_profit_factor: float = 1.2,\n        target_accuracy: float = 0.65,\n        target_bets: float = 90.0\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Dynamically adjust consensus thresholds based on recent performance.\n\n        Prioritizes risk-adjusted returns (Sharpe) and profitability (profit factor).\n        If Sharpe or profit factor are below target, tighten thresholds to improve quality.\n        If accuracy is high but Sharpe is low, also tighten (filter out low-quality trades).\n        If bets are too low and accuracy acceptable, loosen to increase frequency.\n        \"\"\"\n        sharpe = recent_performance.get(\"sharpe\", -1000.0)\n        profit_factor = recent_performance.get(\"profit_factor\", 0.0)\n        accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)\n        bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)\n\n        # Directional accuracy insufficient: tighten to require stronger agreement\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.03)\n        elif bets_per_month < target_bets and accuracy >= target_accuracy:\n            # horizon -> population\n        self.main_features = []  # list of feature names produced by this ensemble\n        self.is_fitted = False\n\n    def fit_horizon_models(\n        self,\n        horizon_data: Dict[str, pd.DataFrame],\n        target_series: pd.Series = None\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Train a separate model population for each horizon.\n\n        Args:\n            horizon_data: dict of {horizon: DataFrame} with features and 'target' column for that horizon\n            target_series: ignored (for backward compatibility)\n        \"\"\"\n        self.horizon_models = {}\n\n        horizons = list(horizon_data.items())\n        print(f\"Fitting horizon ensembles for {len(horizons)} horizons\", flush=True)\n        for idx, (horizon, df) in enumerate(horizons):\n            if df.empty:\n                print(f\"  Horizon {horizon}: empty, skipping\", flush=True)\n                continue\n\n            print(f\"  Horizon {horizon} ({idx+1}/{len(horizons)}): processing {len(df)} rows\", flush=True)\n\n            # Set index for alignment\n            df_indexed = df.set_index(\"open_time\")\n\n            # Use the horizon-specific target from df['target']\n            if 'target' not in df_indexed.columns:\n                print(f\"    WARNING: no 'target' column in horizon data; skipping\", flush=True)\n                continue\n            y = df_indexed['target']\n\n            # Prepare features (exclude time and price/volume and target)\n            exclude_cols = [\"open_time\", \"open\", \"high\", \"low\", \"close\", \"volume\", \"quote_volume\", \"target\", \"future_close\"]\n            feature_cols = [c for c in df_indexed.columns if c not in exclude_cols]\n            X = df_indexed[feature_cols]\n\n            # Drop rows where target is NaN\n            valid_idx = y.notna()\n            if not valid_idx.any():\n                print(f\"    WARNING: all targets NaN; skipping\", flush=True)\n                continue\n            X = X[valid_idx]\n            y = y[valid_idx]\n\n            # Double-check: ensure no NaNs remain in y (some models are sensitive)\n            if y.isna().any():\n                # Drop any remaining NaNs just in case\n                nan_count = y.isna().sum()\n                print(f\"    Warning: {nan_count} NaNs in y after filtering; dropping\", flush=True)\n                X = X[~y.isna()]\n                y = y[~y.isna()]\n\n            print(f\"    Feature count: {len(feature_cols)}, training samples: {len(X)}\", flush=True)\n\n            # Create population (use only random_forest for speed and stability)\n            pop = Population(\n                population_size=5,  # small for horizon models\n                model_types=[\"random_forest\"],\n                elitism_count=1\n            )\n            pop.initialize(input_dim=len(feature_cols), feature_names=feature_cols)\n\n            # Quick training: fit all models\n            print(f\"    Training {len(pop.individuals)} models...\", flush=True)\n            self._train_population(pop, X, y)\n            self.horizon_models[horizon] = pop\n            print(f\"    Completed horizon {horizon}\", flush=True)\n\n        self.is_fitted = True\n        print(\"All horizon ensembles fitted\", flush=True)\n\n    def _train_population(self, population: Population, X: pd.DataFrame, y: pd.Series):\n        \"\"\"Fit all models in a population.\"\"\"\n        total = len(population.individuals)\n        for i, ind in enumerate(population.individuals):\n            try:\n                print(f\"[horizon]   Training model {i+1}/{total} ({ind.model_type})...\", flush=True)\n                ind.model.fit(X, y)\n                print(f\"[horizon]   Model {i+1} trained\", flush=True)\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[horizon]   Model {i+1} failed: {e}\", flush=True)\n                # Set very low fitness if model fails\n                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n    def generate_features(\n        self,\n        horizon_data: Dict[str, pd.DataFrame],\n        base_index: pd.DatetimeIndex\n    ) -> pd.DataFrame:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate horizon ensemble features: predictions from each horizon's best model.\n\n        Returns:\n            DataFrame with columns like: h_1h_pred, h_1h_proba, h_4h_pred, ...\n        \"\"\"\n        if not self.is_fitted:\n            raise RuntimeError(\"HorizonEnsemble must be fitted first\")\n\n        features = pd.DataFrame(index=base_index)\n\n        for horizon, pop in self.horizon_models.items():\n            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n\n            # Get horizon data aligned to base index\n            df_h = horizon_data[horizon].set_index(\"open_time\")\n            X_h = df_h.reindex(base_index)\n\n            # Drop non-feature columns\n            feature_cols = [c for c in X_h.columns if c not in [\"open\", \"high\", \"low\", \"close\", \"volume\", \"quote_volume\"]]\n            X_h_features = X_h[feature_cols]\n\n            # Forward fill any missing features (from resampling gaps)\n            X_h_features = X_h_features.ffill()\n\n            # Generate predictions\n            try:\n                proba = best.model.predict_proba(X_h_features)\n                pred = best.model.predict(X_h_features, threshold=0.5)\n                features[f\"h_{horizon}_proba\"] = proba\n                features[f\"h_{horizon}_pred\"] = pred\n            except Exception as e:\n                # If prediction fails, fill with 0.5 (neutral)\n                features[f\"h_{horizon}_proba\"] = 0.5\n                features[f\"h_{horizon}_pred\"] = 0\n\n        self.main_features = list(features.columns)\n        return features\n\n    def get_feature_names(self) -> List[str]:\n        return self.main_features\n","numLines":157,"startLine":1,"totalLines":157}}}

Combined transaction cost: fee + slippage\n        entry_cost = self.fee_rate + self.slippage\n        exit_cost = self.fee_rate + self.slippage\n\n        # Determine if we have high/low for stop-loss\n        use_stop = self.stop_loss_pct > 0\n        if isinstance(prices, pd.DataFrame):\n            # Expect columns: 'close', optionally 'high', 'low'\n            if 'high' in prices.columns and 'low' in prices.columns:\n                close_series = prices['close']\n                high_series = prices['high']\n                low_series = prices['low']\n            else:\n                close_series = prices['close']\n                high_series = low_series = close_series\n        else:\n            close_series = prices\n            high_series = low_series = prices\n\n        # Align signals and prices\n        signals = signals.reindex(close_series.index).fillna(-1)\n\n        # Build equity curve indexed by signals.index\n        equity = pd.Series(index=signals.index, dtype=float)\n        equity.iloc[0] = capital\n\n        # Iterate through each timestamp, use signal to open a trade that closes at next timestamp\n        for i in range(len(signals) - 1):\n            sig = signals.iloc[i]\n            current_price = close_series.iloc[i]\n            next_close = close_series.iloc[i+1]\n            next_high = high_series.iloc[i+1]\n            next_low = low_series.iloc[i+1]\n\n            if sig == -1:\n                # No trade, carry forward capital\n                equity.iloc[i+1] = capital\n                continue\n\n            # Determine entry price with cost\n            if sig == 1:  # long\n                entry = current_price * (1 + entry_cost)\n                # Determine exit price considering stop-loss\n                stop_price = entry * (1 - self.stop_loss_pct) if use_stop else None\n                exit_price = next_close * (1 - exit_cost)\n                if use_stop and next_low <= stop_price:\n                    # Stop triggered: exit at stop price (with exit cost)\n                    exit_price = stop_price * (1 - exit_cost)\n                ret = (exit_price / entry) - 1\n            else:  # short\n                entry = current_price * (1 - entry_cost)\n                stop_price = entry * (1 + self.stop_loss_pct) if use_stop else None\n                exit_price = next_close * (1 + exit_cost)\n                if use_stop and next_high >= stop_price:\n                    exit_price = stop_price * (1 + exit_cost)\n                ret = (entry / exit_price) - 1\n\n            # Apply bet size\n            capital *= (1 + ret * self.bet_size)\n\n            self.trades.append({\n                \"entry_time\": signals.index[i],\n                \"exit_time\": signals.index[i+1],\n                \"entry_price\": entry,\n                \"exit_price\": exit_price,\n                \"return\": ret,\n                \"pnl\": capital - self.initial_capital,\n                \"stopped\": use_stop and ((sig == 1 and next_low <= stop_price) or (sig == 0 and next_high >= stop_price))\n            })\n\n            equity.iloc[i+1] = capital\n\n        # Fill any remaining NaNs in equity with last value\n        equity = equity.ffill()\n\n        self.equity_curve = equity\n\n        # Calculate metrics\n        self.metrics = self._compute_metrics()\n\n        return self.metrics\n\n    def _compute_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"Compute metrics from simulation.\"\"\"\n        if not self.trades:\n            return {\n                \"accuracy\": 0.0,\n                \"bets_per_month\": 0.0,\n                \"sharpe\": 0.0,\n                \"max_drawdown\": 0.0,\n                \"total_return\": 0.0,\n                \"n_trades\": 0,\n                \"profit_factor\": 0.0,\n                \"final_equity\": self.initial_capital\n            }\n\n        returns = [t[\"return\"] for t in self.trades]\n        winning = sum(1 for r in returns if r > 0)\n        accuracy = winning / len(returns)\n\n        # Bets per month (entries)\n        n_entries = len(self.trades)\n        if self.equity_curve is not None and len(self.equity_curve) > 0:\n            period_days = len(self.equity_curve) / (24 * 4)  # 15-min candles to days\n        else:\n            period_days = 0\n        months = period_days / 30.44\n        bets_per_month = n_entries / months if months > 0 else 0\n\n        # Sharpe\n        if self.equity_curve is not None:\n            eq_returns = self.equity_curve.pct_change().dropna()\n            if eq_returns.std() > 0:\n                sharpe = (eq_returns.mean() / eq_returns.std()) * np.sqrt(365 * 24 * 4)\n            else:\n                sharpe = 0.0\n\n            # Max drawdown\n            running_max = self.equity_curve.expanding().max()\n            drawdown = (self.equity_curve - running_max) / running_max\n            max_drawdown = abs(drawdown.min())\n        else:\n            sharpe = 0.0\n            max_drawdown = 0.0\n\n        total_return = (self.equity_curve.iloc[-1] - self.initial_capital) / self.initial_capital\n\n        gross_profit = sum(r for r in returns if r > 0)\n        gross_loss = abs(sum(r for r in returns if r < 0))\n        profit_factor = gross_profit / (gross_loss + 1e-10)\n\n        return {\n            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n            \"bets_per_month\": bets_per_month,\n            \"sharpe\": sharpe,\n            \"max_drawdown\": max_drawdown,\n            \"total_return\": total_return,\n            \"n_trades\": len(self.trades),\n            \"profit_factor\": profit_factor,\n            \"final_equity\": self.equity_curve.iloc[-1] if self.equity_curve is not None else self.initial_capital,\n            \"gross_profit\": gross_profit,\n            \"gross_loss\": gross_loss\n        }\n\n    def get_equity_curve(self) -> pd.Series:\n        return self.equity_curve\n\n    def get_trades(self) -> pd.DataFrame:\n        return pd.DataFrame(self.trades)\n","numLines":204,"startLine":1,"totalLines":204}}}

If extremely few trades (or none), loosen to generate activity\n        if bets_per_month < 30.0:\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n            # After loosening for low activity, skip further adjustments this cycle\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n            return\n\n        # Primary: Sharpe and profitability\n        if sharpe < target_sharpe or profit_factor < target_profit_factor:\n            # Poor risk-adjusted/absolute performance: tighten to filter trades\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = min(5, self.min_models_agree + 1)\n        elif accuracy < target_accuracy:\n            # Directional accuracy insufficient: tighten to require stronger agreement\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.03)\n        elif bets_per_month < target_bets and accuracy >= target_accuracy:\n            # No model worked, all NO_TRADE\n            signals[:] = -1\n            return signals\n\n        probas_array = np.array(probas_matrix)  # shape: (n_models, n_samples)\n\n        # Average confidence for each sample\n        avg_proba = probas_array.mean(axis=0)\n\n        # Count models predicting UP\n        up_votes = (probas_array >= 0.5).sum(axis=0)\n\n        down_votes = len(probas_matrix) - up_votes\n\n        # Apply gating rules\n        for i, (avg_p, up, down) in enumerate(zip(avg_proba, up_votes, down_votes)):\n            # Check agreement\n            if up >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 1\n                confidence = avg_p\n            elif down >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 0\n                confidence = 1 - avg_p  # confidence in DOWN is 1 - avg_proba\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n                continue\n\n            # Check confidence threshold\n            if confidence >= self.min_confidence:\n                signals.iloc[i] = direction\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n\n        return signals\n\n    def adjust_thresholds(\n        self,\n        recent_performance: Dict[str, float],\n        target_sharpe: float = 1.0,\n        target_profit_factor: float = 1.2,\n        target_accuracy: float = 0.65,\n        target_bets: float = 90.0\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Dynamically adjust consensus thresholds based on recent performance.\n\n        Prioritizes risk-adjusted returns (Sharpe) and profitability (profit factor).\n        If Sharpe or profit factor are below target, tighten thresholds to improve quality.\n        If accuracy is high but Sharpe is low, also tighten (filter out low-quality trades).\n        If bets are too low and accuracy acceptable, loosen to increase frequency.\n        \"\"\"\n        sharpe = recent_performance.get(\"sharpe\", -1000.0)\n        profit_factor = recent_performance.get(\"profit_factor\", 0.0)\n        accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)\n        bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)\n\n        # Primary: Sharpe and profitability\n        if sharpe < target_sharpe or profit_factor < target_profit_factor:\n            # Poor risk-adjusted/absolute performance: tighten to filter trades\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = min(5, self.min_models_agree + 1)\n        elif accuracy < target_accuracy:\n            # Directional accuracy insufficient: tighten to require stronger agreement\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.03)\n        elif bets_per_month < target_bets and accuracy >= target_accuracy:\n            # Too few trades despite decent accuracy: loosen thresholds\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.02)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n        # else: keep thresholds stable\n\n        # Clamp to reasonable ranges\n        self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n        self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n\n    def get_params(self) -> dict:\n        return {\n            \"min_models_agree\": self.min_models_agree,\n            \"min_confidence\": self.min_confidence\n        }\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":108,"oldLines":6,"newStart":108,"newLines":15,"lines":["         accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)","         bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)"," ","+        # At least MIN_MODELS_AGREE models must agree on direction\n    - Average confidence must exceed MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        min_models_agree: int = ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n        min_confidence: float = ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    ):\n        self.min_models_agree = min_models_agree\n        self.min_confidence = min_confidence\n\n    def decide(\n        self,\n        models: List[Individual],\n        X: pd.DataFrame\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate final trading signals (UP=1, DOWN=0, NO_TRADE=-1).\n\n        Args:\n            models: list of trained model individuals\n            X: feature DataFrame to predict on\n\n        Returns:\n            Series of signals (1, 0, or -1) aligned to X.index\n        \"\"\"\n        signals = pd.Series(index=X.index, data=0)\n        probas_matrix = []\n\n        for ind in models:\n            try:\n                proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X)\n                probas_matrix.append(proba)\n            except Exception as e:\n                continue\n\n        if not probas_matrix:\n            # No model worked, all NO_TRADE\n            signals[:] = -1\n            return signals\n\n        probas_array = np.array(probas_matrix)  # shape: (n_models, n_samples)\n\n        # Average confidence for each sample\n        avg_proba = probas_array.mean(axis=0)\n\n        # Count models predicting UP\n        up_votes = (probas_array >= 0.5).sum(axis=0)\n\n        down_votes = len(probas_matrix) - up_votes\n\n        # Apply gating rules\n        for i, (avg_p, up, down) in enumerate(zip(avg_proba, up_votes, down_votes)):\n            # Check agreement\n            if up >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 1\n                confidence = avg_p\n            elif down >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 0\n                confidence = 1 - avg_p  # confidence in DOWN is 1 - avg_proba\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n                continue\n\n            # Check confidence threshold\n            if confidence >= self.min_confidence:\n                signals.iloc[i] = direction\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n\n        return signals\n\n    def adjust_thresholds(\n        self,\n        recent_performance: Dict[str, float],\n        target_sharpe: float = 1.0,\n        target_profit_factor: float = 1.2,\n        target_accuracy: float = 0.65,\n        target_bets: float = 90.0\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Dynamically adjust consensus thresholds based on recent performance.\n\n        Prioritizes risk-adjusted returns (Sharpe) and profitability (profit factor).\n        If Sharpe or profit factor are below target, tighten thresholds to improve quality.\n        If accuracy is high but Sharpe is low, also tighten (filter out low-quality trades).\n        If bets are too low and accuracy acceptable, loosen to increase frequency.\n        \"\"\"\n        sharpe = recent_performance.get(\"sharpe\", -1000.0)\n        profit_factor = recent_performance.get(\"profit_factor\", 0.0)\n        accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)\n        bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)\n\n        # If extremely few trades (or none), loosen to generate activity\n        if bets_per_month < 30.0:\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n            # After loosening for low activity, skip further adjustments this cycle\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n            return\n\n        # Primary: Sharpe and profitability\n        if sharpe < target_sharpe or profit_factor < target_profit_factor:\n            # Poor risk-adjusted/absolute performance: tighten to filter trades\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = min(5, self.min_models_agree + 1)\n        elif accuracy < target_accuracy:\n            # Directional accuracy insufficient: tighten to require stronger agreement\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.03)\n        elif bets_per_month < target_bets and accuracy >= target_accuracy:\n            # Too few trades despite decent accuracy: loosen thresholds\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.02)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n        # else: keep thresholds stable\n\n        # Clamp to reasonable ranges\n        self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n        self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n\n    def get_params(self) -> dict:\n        return {\n            \"min_models_agree\": self.min_models_agree,\n            \"min_confidence\": self.min_confidence\n        }\n","numLines":143,"startLine":1,"totalLines":143}}}
